Please follow the instructions in the request for evidence. If you do not receive your request for evidence by December 23, 2022, please go to www.uscis.gov/e-request to request a copy of the notice. If you move, go to www.uscis.gov/addresschange to give us your new mailing address.

Please follow the instructions in the request for evidence. If you do not receive your request for evidence by December 23, 2022, please go to www.uscis.gov/e-request to request a copy of the notice. If you move, go to www.uscis.gov/addresschange to give us your new mailing address.
